203:        ``create_pairing_qr(sender_broker_url=...)``.
204:
205:        Signs the literal ASCII bytes ``"syncler-v1-bootstrap-key:"``
206:        (24 bytes) concatenated with the raw 32-byte X25519 public key,
207:        per `docs/crypto-spec.md ֲ§9.1`. Returns the base64
208:        ``bootstrap_key_id`` (server-computed SHA-256(pub)[:16]).
209:        """
210:        self._require_sender_id()
211:        if len(bootstrap_public_key_raw) != 32:
212:            raise ValueError("bootstrap_public_key_raw must be 32 bytes")
213:        sig_input = b"syncler-v1-bootstrap-key:" + bootstrap_public_key_raw
214:        signature = self.private_key.sign(sig_input)
215:        body = {
216:            "sender_id": self._canonical_sender_id(),
217:            "bootstrap_key": b64(bootstrap_public_key_raw),
218:            "bootstrap_key_signature": b64(signature),
219:        }
220:        resp = self.session.post(
221:            f"{self.base_url}/v1/senders/me/bootstrap-key", json=body, timeout=10,
222:        )
223:        resp.raise_for_status()
224:        return resp.json()["bootstrap_key_id"]
225:
226:    def wait_for_pairing(
227:        self,
228:        *,
229:        timeout_seconds: int = 120,
230:        poll_interval_seconds: float = 1.0,
231:    ) -> Pairing:
232:        """V1.5 Phase 5a-2: poll the broker storage until the device's
233:        bootstrap POST lands, then automatically set the pairing on
234:        this client.
235:
236:        Defaults: 120s timeout, 1s poll with ֲ±20% jitter (jitter avoids
237:        synchronized polling when multiple pairings are in flight).
238:        Raises ``TimeoutError`` on deadline. Caller must have wired a
239:        broker storage via ``Client(...)``'s constructor ג€” otherwise
240:        there's nothing to poll.
241:        """
242:        import random
243:        if self._broker_storage is None:
244:            raise SynclerError(
245:                "wait_for_pairing requires a broker storage. Pass one to "
246:                "Client(broker_storage=InMemoryBrokerStorage()) at construction time.",
247:            )
248:        if self._pending_pairing_id is None:
249:            raise SynclerError(
250:                "no pending pairing ג€” call create_pairing_qr(sender_broker_url=...) first",
251:            )
252:        deadline = time.monotonic() + timeout_seconds
253:        while True:
254:            entry = self._broker_storage.fetch(self._pending_pairing_id)
255:            if entry is not None:
256:                pairing = Pairing(
257:                    pairing_id=self._pending_pairing_id,
258:                    user_id=entry.user_id,
259:                )
260:                self._latest_pairing = pairing

codex
Item 1 — Android UX: YELLOW

- `PairingRepository.postBootstrapEnvelope()` documents retrying `429`, but the implementation treats all 4xx as terminal. The stated plan says terminal on 4xx, so code is acceptable; the comment is misleading.
- `PairingScreen.kt:110` decodes `senderPublicKey` outside a guarded path. A malformed preview can crash instead of becoming `BootstrapHardError`.
- Android tests were not run, so this remains YELLOW until Gradle compiles the new Hilt/Retrofit wiring.

Item 2 — FastAPI broker: RED

- `sdk-python/syncler/bootstrap.py:149-150` can raise non-`BootstrapDecryptError` exceptions for attacker-controlled but length-valid X25519 public keys, e.g. low-order/invalid points. `sdk-python/syncler/broker/app.py:227-240` only maps `BootstrapDecryptError` to opaque `401`, so this can become a public `500` instead of the promised opaque decrypt failure.
- Missing test: valid-shape envelope with a 32-byte invalid/low-order `ephemeral_pubkey` must return `401`, not `500`.
- Packaging footgun: new broker tests import FastAPI, but `sdk-python[dev]` does not include the `broker` extra. A clean dev install may not be able to run the full SDK test suite.

Item 3 — Docs: RED

- `docs/integration-guide.md:616` calls `client.set_bootstrap_keypair(...)`, but `Client` has no such method.
- `docs/integration-guide.md:627` calls `wait_for_pairing(timeout=120)`, but the API parameter is `timeout_seconds`.
- `docs/integration-guide.md:628` uses `pairing.pairing_key`, but `Pairing` only contains `pairing_id` and `user_id`; the key is stored on `client.pairing_key`.

Missing from consult 88 dual-GREEN plan:

- Broker test for invalid 32-byte X25519 public input returning opaque `401`.
- Docs must be reconciled with the actual SDK API.
- Prefer at least one Android repository/viewmodel test for automated classification/signature failure/fallback paths, not only DTO serialization.

Commit-readiness vote: NO.
